    <script type="text/javascript">
        /* Checks if a url belongs to the same domain */
        function isLocalUrl(url) {
            return url.startsWith('/') || url.startsWith(location.host, url.indexOf('://') + 3);
        };

        if (!globalThis.loopnet) {
            globalThis.loopnet = {}
        }

        if (!globalThis.loopnet.originalXhrOpen) {
            globalThis.loopnet.originalXhrOpen = XMLHttpRequest.prototype.open;
        }

        if (!globalThis.loopnet.originalXhrSetRequestHeader) {
            globalThis.loopnet.originalXhrSetRequestHeader = XMLHttpRequest.prototype.setRequestHeader;
        }

        // Overrides the setRequestHeader method to to prevent setting csrf token more then once
        XMLHttpRequest.prototype.setRequestHeader = function (header, value) {

            if (globalThis.forge !== undefined &&
                globalThis.forge.csrfHeaderName !== undefined &&
                header === globalThis.forge.csrfHeaderName) {
                    if (!this.csrfTokenSet) {
                        this.csrfTokenSet = true;
                    } else {
                        return;
                    }
            }

            return globalThis.loopnet.originalXhrSetRequestHeader.call(this, header, value);
        };

        // Setting CSRF token header for every XMLHttpRequest instance
        XMLHttpRequest.prototype.open = function() {
            const xhr = this;
            globalThis.loopnet.originalXhrOpen.apply(this, arguments);
            if (arguments.length >= 1 && isLocalUrl(arguments[1])) {
                const forge = globalThis.forge;
                if (forge !== undefined &&
                    forge.csrfHeaderName !== undefined &&
                    forge.csrfTokenValue !== undefined) {
                    xhr.setRequestHeader(forge.csrfHeaderName, forge.csrfTokenValue);
                }
            }
        };

With a proven track record of excellence, a dedicated fan base, and a mouthwatering menu, Hubcap Grill is poised for expansion. Here’s why investing in a Hubcap Grill franchise is a recipe for success...    UNMATCHED FLAVOR &a; QUALITY  Hubcap Grill has built its reputation on crafting burgers that are truly exceptional. Our commitment to using the freshest, highest-quality ingredients shines through in every bite. From locally sourced beef to homemade sauces and hand-selected toppings, our menu is a celebration of flavor that keeps customers coming back for more.    A WINNING BRAND CONCEPT  Hubcap Grill has become an iconic name in Houston’s culinary scene and a local favorite since inception, earning a dedicated following and rave reviews from loyal customers and visitors alike. By becoming a franchise owner, you’ll be part of a brand that has already achieved remarkable success and recognition. Our unique concept, coupled with our dedication to creating an unforgettable dining experience, sets Hubcap Grill apart from the competition.    COMPREHENSIVE TRAINING &a; SUPPORT  As a Hubcap Grill franchise owner, you’ll benefit from our comprehensive support system. We’ll provide you with extensive training, equipping you with the knowledge and skills needed to run a successful restaurant. From site selection and restaurant design to marketing strategies and operational support, our team will be by your side every step of the way.    PROVEN BUSINESS MODEL  Hubcap Grill has a proven business model that has allowed us to thrive in a competitive food industry. We have fine-tuned our operations, ensuring efficiency and profitability. By joining our franchise network, you’ll benefit from our experience, systems, and processes that have been refined over years of successful operations.
